BRTUL ZHUGS MA SMAD PA, ,SROG LAS GCES PAR 'DZIN GYUR CIG ,LUS
DANG SROG LA MI BLTA BAR, ,DUS GSUM RGYAL BA THAMS CAD KYI, ,

LUNG RTOGS DAM CHOS MA LUS PA, ,RGYAL BA'I DGONGS PA JI BZHIN
'DZIN, ,THOG MA MED NAS DRIN BSKYANGS PA'I, ,MAR GYUR 'GRO BA'I
DON GYI PHYIR, ,RIN CHEN BYANG CHUB SEMS BSKYED NAS, ,RLABS CHEN
SPYOD

PA MTHA' DAG BSGRUB, ,DUS GSUM RGYAL BA SRAS BCAS KYI, ,MDZAD PA
RNAM THAR MA LUS PA, ,GCIG TU BSDUS NAS BDAG NYID KYIS, ,'GRO
GNAS BAR DU SPYOD GYUR CIG ,'GRO KUN SNYING GI BU GCIG LTAR,
,MTHONG

NAS DE DAG SGROL BA'I PHYIR, ,BSKAL PAR MNAR MED ME NANG DU,
,'JUG LA'ANG SKYO BA MED GYUR CIG ,MAR GYUR 'GRO BA MTHA' DAG GI
,SDIG DANG SDUG BSNGAL RGUD PA KUN, ,THAMS CAD BDAG GIS LEN

NUS SHING, ,CIG CAR BDAG LA SMIN GYUR CIG ,BDAG GI DUS GSUM BDE
DGE RNAMS, ,MAR GYUR SEMS CAN THAMS CAD LA, ,DA LTA NYID DU SMIN
GYUR NAS, ,PHAN BDE'I DPAL GYIS 'BYOR GYUR CIG ,

@320B BDAG LAS DAM CHOS THOS PA DANG, ,DAD CING MOS PA THAMS CAD
LA, ,BYANG CHUB SNYING POR MCHIS KYI BAR, ,YID BZHIN NOR LTAR
'DOD PA BSGRUB, ,BDAG NI MTHONG DANG THOS PA DANG, ,DRAN REG
GYUR PA THAMS CAD

KYANG; ;NGAN 'GROR NAM YANG MI LTUNG ZHING, ,RTAG TU DAM CHOS
SPYOD GYUR CIG ,'DI LTAR BSKRUN PA'I DGE BA'I TSOGS, ,ZLA LTAR
DKAR BA BSAGS PA DES, ,STON MCHOG SH'AKYA'I GTZO BO DES, ,BDAG
CAG

'BRAL MED 'DZIN GYUR CIG ,DPAL LDAN 'DOD KHAMS DBANG PHYUG MAR,
,LHA RDZAS NA BZA' 'DI PHUL BAS, ,DENG NAS BYANG CHUB CHEN PO'I
BAR, ,GA-YEL MED MGON DANG SKYABS MDZOD CIG ,'DOD KHAMS DBANG

BSGYUR DPA' MO CHE'I, ,THUGS RJE BSIL BA'I CHU RGYUN GYIS, ,BDAG
CAG DENG 'DIR MNGON 'DOD PA'I, ,GSER GYI RDZING BU GANG BAR
MDZOD,, ,,*, ,NA MO GU RU MANYDZU GHO sh'A YA,,

RGYAL BA'I YAB GCIG RJE BTZUN MKHYEN PA'I GTER, ,NGUR SMRIG GAR
GYIS RNAM ROL TZONG KHA PA, ,BSLU MED SKYABS GSUM 'DUS PA'I BDAG
NYID DU, ,GSOL BA 'DEBS SO BRTZE PA'I LCAGS KYUS ZUNGS, ,SA

YI DPAL MO KHYOD LA BDAG GIS NI, ,THUB PA'I DBANG PO'I GSUNG RAB
LAS BYUNG BA'I, ,SDEBS LEGS TSIG GI ME TOG PHRENG MDZES PA,
,CUNG ZAD SPEL 'DI MGUL BA'I RGYAN DU 'BUL, ,SNGON CHAD RNAM
DKAR
@321A *, ,DAG PA'I LAS BSAGS PAS, ,DA LTA RIGS MTHO YID 'ONG
GZUGS MDZES LDAN, ,PHUN TSOGS 'BYOR PA NAM MKHA'I MDZOD BRNYES
SHING, ,KUN GYIS BKUR BA'I GNAS SU GYUR PA

LAGS, ,DA YANG SPU GRI'I SOR CHAGS SBRANG RTZI LTAR, ,MNOG CHUNG
NYES PA KUN GYI GZHIR GYUR PA'I, ,TSE 'DI'I BDE LA CHES CHER MA
ZHEN PAR, ,PHYI MA'I DON DU SGO GSUM DGE LA 'BUNGS, ,LAS KYI
DBANG

GIS 'KHOR BAR 'KHYAMS PA'I TSE, ,DKON MCHOG GSUM LAS LHAG PA'I
SKYABS MED PAS, ,GLO SNYING BRANG GSUM GTAD PA'I SKYABS 'GRO
DANG, ,MCHOD SPRIN RGYA MTSOS RGYUN TU MCHOD PAR MDZOD, ,CHOS

KYI SNYING PO GZHAN GYI DON BYED PAR, ,BDE GSHEGS SRAS DANG BCAS
PAS LEGS PAR BSNGAGS, ,DE'I PHYIR CHAGS SDANG SPANGS NAS SKYE
DGU KUN, ,DPAL DANG LDAN PA KHYOD KYIS BU BZHIN SKYONG, ,LONGS

SPYOD GA-YO BA SBRANG MA'I SBRANG RTZI BZHIN, ,SER SNAS BSAGS
KYANG NGES PA 'GA' MA MCHIS, ,RANG DBANG YOD DUS SBYIN PA CHER
BSTZAL NA, ,RANG GI PHYI MA'I NOR SKAL GSOG PA YIN, ,LANG TSO'I
DPAL YANG STON

KA'I ME TOG LTAR, ,RING POR MI THOGS YUD KYIS RNYINGS 'GYUR
ZHING, ,'CHI BDAG BDUD DE NYI RGAS GRIB SO BZHIN, ,SKAD CIG RE
YANG MI SDOD TSUR TSUR 'ONG, ,DE'I PHYIR LUS DANG LONGS SPYOD
KUN BOR NAS, ,DBANG

@321B MED 'JIG RTEN PHA ROL 'GRO BA'I TSE, ,CHOS LAS GZHAN GYIS
PHAN PA CAD MED NA, ,DA LTA NYID NAS TSUL BZHIN BSGRUBS NA LEGS,
,NYA STONG TSES BRGYAD CHOS 'PHRUL ZLA BA SOGS, ,DUS BZANG RNAMS
LA GSO

SBYONG YAN LAG BRGYAD, ,BZHES PAR MDZOD CIG LHA MI'I RTEN BZANG
PO, ,BRGYUD NAS RIM GYIS MYA NGAN 'DAS PA 'THOB, ,LHA DANG BLA
MA THONG BZHIN BSTEN PA DANG, ,'BANGS RNAMS BYAMS PA'I THUGS
KYIS SKYONG

BA DANG, ,CHOS KYI RGYAL SRID SKYONG BA'I BYA BA GSUM, ,PHAN
TSUN 'GRAN PA BZHIN DU KHYOD KYIS SGRUBS, ,'BYOR BA'I TSE NA
DREGS PAR MI BYA ZHING, ,RGUD NA'ANG HA CANG ZHUM PAR MI BYA
STE, ,'KHOR BA'I GNAS 'DIR YID

BRTAN MA MCHIS PAS, ,LAS 'BRAS TSUL LA RTAG TU SEMS PAR MDZOD,
,MDOR NA BDAG GIS MANG DU GSOL CI 'TSAL, ,PHAN PA'I GDAMS NGAG
GTZO BO 'DI YIN TE, ,NYID KYI SRAS BZHIN SKYE DGU MA

LUS PA, ,BYAMS PA'I THUGS KYIS KUN TU SKYONG BAR MDZOD, ,'DOD
CHAGS ZHE SDANG GTI MUG RNAM PA GSUM, ,SDUG BSNGAL KUN GYI RTZA
BAR RGYAL BAS GSUNGS, ,DE'I PHYIR 'DI DAG DPAL MO KHYOD NYID
KYIS, ,

YID KYI DGU LA'ANG SEMS PA SPANG BAR BGYI, ,DE LTAR JI SKAD
GDAMS PA'I DON RNAMS KUN, ,NYID KYIS TSUL BZHIN NYAMS SU BZHES
LAGS NA, ,'KHOR BA'I SDUG BSNGAL MA LUS DRUNGS PHYUNG NAS, ,SKYE

@322A *, ,RGA NA 'CHI SPANGS PA'I SKU 'THOB 'GYUR, ,TSUL 'DI DGE

RGYAL MO YI, ,RNAM DKAR LEGS SPYAD BZHED PA BSGRUB PA'I PHYIR,
